
if not game:IsLoaded() then
    game.IsLoaded:Wait()
end

repeat task.wait() until getgenv().Configs
local CFG = getgenv().Configs
local lp = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer

task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        if not lp.Team or lp.Team.Name == "Neutral" then
            pcall(function()
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("CommF_"):InvokeServer("SetTeam","Pirates")
            end)
        else
            break
        end
        task.wait(1)
    end
end)
local ps = game:GetService("Players")
local pi = game.PlaceId
local ws = game:GetService("Workspace")
local es = ws:WaitForChild("Enemies")
local ts = game:GetService("TeleportService")
local rt = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Level = lp:WaitForChild("Data"):WaitForChild("Level")
local Fragments = lp:WaitForChild("Data"):WaitForChild("Fragments")
local Beli = lp:WaitForChild("Data"):WaitForChild("Beli")
local r_Net_0 = require(rt.Modules.Net)
local Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
local vim = game:service('VirtualInputManager')
local vs = game:service('VirtualUser')
local cg = game:GetService("CoreGui")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local mt = {}
task.spawn(function()
    if CFG["Black Screen"] then
       game:GetService('Lighting').ExposureCompensation = -math.huge
    end
end)
task.spawn(function()
    if CFG["Lock Fps"]["Enabled"] then
        local fps = CFG["Lock Fps"]["FPS"]
        while true do
            setfpscap(fps)
        end
    end
end)
task.spawn(function()
    if getgenv().Configs and getgenv().Configs["FPS Booster"] then
        rt.Effect:Destroy()
        for i, v in pairs(getconnections(lp.PlayerGui.Main.Settings.Buttons.FastModeButton.Activated)) do
            v.Function()
        end
    end
end)
wait(2)
task.spawn(function()
    if CFG["FPS Booster"] then
        local enemies = ws:WaitForChild("Enemies")
        local mapParts = ws:WaitForChild("Map"):GetDescendants()
        for _, part in ipairs(mapParts) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                local inProtectedPlate = false
                for i = 1, 5 do
                    local plate = ws.Map.Jungle.QuestPlates:FindFirstChild("Plate" .. i)
                    if plate and part.Name == "Button" and part:IsDescendantOf(plate) then
                        inProtectedPlate = true
                        break
                    end
                end
                if inProtectedPlate then
                    continue
                end
                if part.Name == "Door" and part:IsDescendantOf(ws.Map.Ice) then
                    continue
                end
                if part:IsDescendantOf(ws.Map.Jungle:FindFirstChild("Final")) then
                    continue
                end
                if ws.Map:FindFirstChild("IceCastle") then
                    if part:IsDescendantOf(ws.Map:FindFirstChild("IceCastle")) then
                        continue
                    end
                end
                local safeToDelete = true
                for _, enemy in ipairs(enemies:GetChildren()) do
                    local enemyHRP = enemy:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if enemyHRP and (enemyHRP.Position - part.Position).Magnitude < 10 then
                        safeToDelete = false
                        break
                    end
                end
                if safeToDelete then
                    part:Destroy()
                end
            end
        end
        if lp.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("Notifications") then
            lp.PlayerGui.Notifications.Enabled = false
        end
        shared = shared or {}
        if shared.BC_1 == nil then
            shared.BC_1 = true
        end

        if shared.BC_1 and shared.BC_2 == nil then
            local L_1 = workspace
            local L_2 = Lighting
            local L_3 = L_1.Terrain
            local L_4 = ps
            local L_5 = lp.Character

            L_3.WaterWaveSize = 0
            L_3.WaterWaveSpeed = 0
            L_3.WaterReflectance = 0
            L_3.WaterTransparency = 0

            L_2.GlobalShadows = false
            L_2.FogEnd = 9e9
            L_2.Brightness = 0

            if settings and settings().Rendering then
                settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = "Level01"
                settings().Rendering.GraphicsMode = "NoGraphics"
            end

            for _, v in pairs(L_1:GetDescendants()) do
                if v:IsA("BasePart") or v:IsA("SpawnLocation") or v:IsA("WedgePart") or v:IsA("Terrain") or v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                    v.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
                    v.Reflectance = 0
                    v.CastShadow = false
                elseif v:IsA("Decal") or v:IsA("Texture") then
                    v.Texture = ""
                    v.Transparency = 1
                elseif v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or v:IsA("Trail") then
                    v.LightInfluence = 0
                    v.Texture = ""
                    v.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0)
                elseif v:IsA("Explosion") then
                    v.BlastPressure = 0
                    v.BlastRadius = 0
                elseif v:IsA("Fire") or v:IsA("SpotLight") or v:IsA("Smoke") or v:IsA("Sparkles") then
                    v.Enabled = false
                elseif v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                    v.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
                    v.Reflectance = 0
                    v.TextureID = ""
                    v.CastShadow = false
                    v.RenderFidelity = Enum.RenderFidelity.Performance
                elseif v:IsA("SpecialMesh") then
                    v.TextureId = ""
                elseif v:IsA("Shirt") or v:IsA("Pants") or v:IsA("Accessory") then
                    v:Destroy()
                end
            end

            for _, v in pairs(L_2:GetDescendants()) do
                if v:IsA("BlurEffect") or v:IsA("SunRaysEffect") or v:IsA("ColorCorrectionEffect") or v:IsA("BloomEffect") or v:IsA("DepthOfFieldEffect") then
                    v.Enabled = false
                end
            end

            if L_5 then
                for _, v in pairs(L_5:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("Shirt") or v:IsA("Pants") or v:IsA("Accessory") then
                        v:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
            if pi == 2753915549 or pi == 85211729168715 or pi == 79091703265657 or pi == 100117331123089  or pi == 4442272183 or pi == 7449423635 then
                local effectContainer = rt:FindFirstChild("Effect") and rt.Effect:FindFirstChild("Container")
                if effectContainer then
                    local sharedEffects = effectContainer:FindFirstChild("Shared")
                    local miscEffects = effectContainer:FindFirstChild("Misc")

                    if sharedEffects then
                        if sharedEffects:FindFirstChild("AirDash") then
                            sharedEffects.AirDash:Destroy()
                        end
                        if sharedEffects:FindFirstChild("LightningTP") then
                            sharedEffects.LightningTP:Destroy()
                        end
                    end

                    if miscEffects then
                        if miscEffects:FindFirstChild("Damage") then
                            miscEffects.Damage:Destroy()
                        end
                        if miscEffects:FindFirstChild("Confetti") then
                            miscEffects.Confetti:Destroy()
                        end
                    end

                    if effectContainer:FindFirstChild("LevelUp") then
                        effectContainer.LevelUp:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        shared.BC_2 = true
    end
end)

-- // PREMIUM UI OVERHAUL \\ --
local Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
-- ==========================================
--    NOTIFICATION - TÙY CHỌN VỊ TRÍ
-- ==========================================

local NotificationSystem = {
    notifications = {},
    spacing = 90,
    gui = nil,
    position = "BottomRight" -- "TopRight", "BottomRight", "TopLeft", "BottomLeft"
}

local function CreateGui()
    local player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
    local playerGui = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
    
    if playerGui:FindFirstChild("NotificationSystem") then
        return playerGui:FindFirstChild("NotificationSystem")
    end
    
    local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    screenGui.Name = "NotificationSystem"
    screenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    screenGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
    screenGui.Parent = playerGui
    
    return screenGui
end

NotificationSystem.gui = CreateGui()

function NotificationSystem:GetPosition(index)
    local positions = {
        TopRight = {
            start = UDim2.new(1, 50, 0, 20),
            target = function(i) return UDim2.new(1, -370, 0, 20 + ((i - 1) * self.spacing)) end,
            anchor = Vector2.new(0, 0)
        },
        BottomRight = {
            start = UDim2.new(1, 50, 1, -20),
            target = function(i) return UDim2.new(1, -370, 1, -20 - (i * self.spacing)) end,
            anchor = Vector2.new(0, 1)
        },
        TopLeft = {
            start = UDim2.new(0, -370, 0, 20),
            target = function(i) return UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20 + ((i - 1) * self.spacing)) end,
            anchor = Vector2.new(0, 0)
        },
        BottomLeft = {
            start = UDim2.new(0, -370, 1, -20),
            target = function(i) return UDim2.new(0, 20, 1, -20 - (i * self.spacing)) end,
            anchor = Vector2.new(0, 1)
        }
    }
    
    return positions[self.position] or positions.BottomRight
end

function NotificationSystem:UpdatePositions()
    local posData = self:GetPosition()
    
    for i, notif in ipairs(self.notifications) do
        if notif and notif.Parent then
            notif:TweenPosition(
                posData.target(i),
                Enum.EasingDirection.Out,
                Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,
                0.3,
                true
            )
        end
    end
end

function NotificationSystem:Notify(title, message, duration, notifType)
    duration = duration or 3
    notifType = notifType or "Info"
    
    local colors = {
        Info = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45),
        Success = Color3.fromRGB(34, 139, 34),
        Warning = Color3.fromRGB(255, 165, 0),
        Error = Color3.fromRGB(220, 20, 60)
    }
    
    local bgColor = colors[notifType] or colors.Info
    local posData = self:GetPosition()
    
    local notification = Instance.new("Frame")
    notification.Name = "Notification"
    notification.Size = UDim2.new(0, 350, 0, 80)
    notification.Position = posData.start
    notification.AnchorPoint = posData.anchor
    notification.BackgroundColor3 = bgColor
    notification.BorderSizePixel = 0
    notification.Parent = self.gui
    
    local corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
    corner.Parent = notification
    
    local stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    stroke.Thickness = 1
    stroke.Transparency = 0.8
    stroke.Parent = notification
    
    local titleLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    titleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0, 25)
    titleLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 10)
    titleLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    titleLabel.Text = title
    titleLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    titleLabel.TextSize = 14
    titleLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    titleLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    titleLabel.Parent = notification
    
    local messageLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    messageLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0, 35)
    messageLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 35)
    messageLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    messageLabel.Text = message
    messageLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)
    messageLabel.TextSize = 13
    messageLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
    messageLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    messageLabel.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top
    messageLabel.TextWrapped = true
    messageLabel.Parent = notification
    
    local closeButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
    closeButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 30)
    closeButton.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 5)
    closeButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    closeButton.Text = "×"
    closeButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)
    closeButton.TextSize = 24
    closeButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    closeButton.Parent = notification
    
    closeButton.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        closeButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    end)
    
    closeButton.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        closeButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)
    end)
    
    table.insert(self.notifications, notification)
    self:UpdatePositions()
    
    local function closeNotification()
        for i, notif in ipairs(self.notifications) do
            if notif == notification then
                table.remove(self.notifications, i)
                break
            end
        end
        
        notification:TweenPosition(
            posData.start,
            Enum.EasingDirection.In,
            Enum.EasingStyle.Back,
            0.3,
            true,
            function()
                notification:Destroy()
                self:UpdatePositions()
            end
        )
    end
    
    closeButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(closeNotification)
    
    if duration > 0 then
        task.delay(duration, function()
            if notification and notification.Parent then
                closeNotification()
            end
        end)
    end
end

_G.Notify = NotificationSystem

function notify(title, msg, time, type)
    _G.Notify:Notify(title, msg, time or 3, type or "Info")
end

-- // TOGGLE BUTTON \\ --
local ToggleGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
ToggleGui.Name = "ToggleGui"
ToggleGui.Parent = game:GetService("CoreGui")

local ToggleBtnFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
ToggleBtnFrame.Name = "ToggleButtonFrame"
ToggleBtnFrame.Parent = ToggleGui
ToggleBtnFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
ToggleBtnFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0.1, -6)
ToggleBtnFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 50, 0, 50)
ToggleBtnFrame.Active = true
ToggleBtnFrame.Draggable = true

local ToggleCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
ToggleCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
ToggleCorner.Parent = ToggleBtnFrame

local ToggleIcon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
ToggleIcon.Parent = ToggleBtnFrame
ToggleIcon.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
ToggleIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
ToggleIcon.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
ToggleIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, 40)
ToggleIcon.Image = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=107501927776354" --95822296675070

local ToggleButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
ToggleButton.Parent = ToggleBtnFrame
ToggleButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
ToggleButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
ToggleButton.Text = ""

ToggleButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    MainGui.Enabled = not MainGui.Enabled
    if MainGui.Enabled then
        TweenService:Create(BlurEffect, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {Size = 24}):Play()
        TweenService:Create(ToggleBtnFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.25}):Play()
    else
        TweenService:Create(BlurEffect, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {Size = 0}):Play()
        TweenService:Create(ToggleBtnFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
    end
end)

function UpdateStatusItem(p)
    StatusItemLabel.Text = "Status : " .. tostring(p)
end

function UpdateStatusAccount(p)
    if StatusItemLabel.Text == "Status : Initializing..." or StatusItemLabel.Text == "Status: Initializing..." then
        UpdateStatusItem("Farming")
    end
    StatusFarmLabel.Text = "Status Farm : " .. tostring(p)
end

function UpdateStatusMob(p)
    StatusMobLabel.Text = "Farm Mob : " .. tostring(p)
end

Stats = {
    Status = {
        SetTitle = function(self, text)
            UpdateStatusAccount(text)
        end,
        SetMob = function(self, text)
            UpdateStatusMob(text)
        end
    }
}

_G.UpdateStatusAccount = UpdateStatusAccount
_G.UpdateStatusItem = UpdateStatusItem
_G.UpdateStatusMob = UpdateStatusMob

local Tween
function TPZ(p)
    local Distance = (p.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
    local Speed
    if Distance < 100 then
        Speed = 50
    elseif Distance < 400 then
        Speed = 400
    elseif Distance < 1000 then
        Speed = 300
    elseif Distance < 1500 then
        Speed = 260
    elseif Distance >= 1500 then
        Speed = 300
    end
    Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart,
        TweenInfo.new(Distance / Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),
        {CFrame = p}
    )
    Tween:Play()
end
local Tween
local LastTPTime = tick()
local lp = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer

local function StopTP()
    if Tween then
        Tween:Cancel()
        Tween = nil
    end
end

local function tp(RealTarget, d, D)
    local speed = 300
    if d == 1.6 then speed = 350 end
    local Dis = D or 130
    local hrp = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    local humanoid = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    if not hrp or not humanoid then return end
    local Distance = (RealTarget.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
    if Distance > 3000 and humanoid.Health > 0 then
        local portals = {
            {Vector3.new(61163.85, 11.67, 1819.78), "Old_World"},
            {Vector3.new(-4607.82, 872.54, -1667.55), "Old_World"},
            {Vector3.new(-7894.61, 5547.14, -380.29), "Old_World"},
            {Vector3.new(923.21, 126.97, 32852.83), "New_World"},
            {Vector3.new(-2953.31, 41.01, 2099.17), "Old_World"},
        }
        for _, v in pairs(portals) do
            if _G[v[2]] and (v[1] - RealTarget.Position).Magnitude <= 2300 then
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("requestEntrance", v[1])
                break
            end
        end
    end
    -- Reset TP Mechanism (10s interval)
    if not _G.LastTpReset or tick() - _G.LastTpReset > 10 then
        _G.LastTpReset = tick()
        local Offset = CFrame.new(math.random(-2, 2), 0, math.random(-2, 2))
        RealTarget = RealTarget * Offset
    end

    LastTPTime = tick()
    StopTP()
    local distance = (RealTarget.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position.X, RealTarget.Position.Y, hrp.Position.Z)
    if distance < 130 then
        pcall(function()
            hrp.CFrame = RealTarget
        end)
        return
    elseif distance < Dis then
        speed = 350
    end
    for _, child in pairs(lp.Character:GetDescendants()) do
        if child:IsA("BasePart") and child.CanCollide then
            child.CanCollide = false
        end
    end
    
    local duration = distance / speed
    local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(duration, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
    local goal = {CFrame = RealTarget}
    Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(hrp, tweenInfo, goal)
    Tween:Play()
end

local function Ew()
    if God_Human_C_M then
        local Inventory = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")
        for _, v in pairs(Inventory) do
            if v.Type == "Sword" then
                if v.Name == "Tushita" and v.Mastery >= 400 then
                    Tushita_M = true
                elseif v.Name == "Yama" and v.Mastery >= 400 then
                    Yama_M = true
                end
            end
        end
        if not Tushita_M then
            if not mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, "Tushita") and not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Tushita") then
                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LoadItem","Tushita")
            end
        elseif not Yama_M then
            if not mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, "Yama") and not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Yama") then
                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LoadItem","Yama")
            end
        end
        for _, v in pairs(lp.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
            if v:IsA("Tool") and tostring(v.ToolTip) == "Sword" then
                lp.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid"):EquipTool(v)
            end
        end
    else
        for _, v in pairs(lp.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
            if v:IsA("Tool") and tostring(v.ToolTip) == "Melee" then
                lp.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid"):EquipTool(v)
            end
        end
    end
end
function TPBoat(p,boat,speedx,stop)
    if stop == nil then
        stop = false
    end
    local Distance = (p.Position - boat.Position).Magnitude
    Speed = speedx
    TweenP = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(boat,TweenInfo.new(Distance/Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{CFrame = p})
    if stop == true then
        TweenP:Cancel()
    else
        TweenP:Play()
    end
end

setmetatable(mt, {
    __index = function(_, k)
        if k == "wt" then
            return function(p)
                return task.wait(p)
            end
        elseif k == "p" then
            return function(...)
                return pcall(...)
            end
        elseif k == "sf" then
            return function(o, c)
                return string.find(o, tostring(c))
            end
        elseif k == "cf" then
            return function(...)
                lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(...)
            end
        elseif k == "ffc" then
            return function(o, c)
                return o and o:FindFirstChild(c)
            end
        elseif k == "Equip" then
            return function(toolName)
                if not toolName or type(toolName) ~= "string" then return end
                for _, v in pairs(lp.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
                    if v:IsA("Tool") and v.Name == toolName then
                        lp.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid"):EquipTool(v)
                    end
                end
            end
        elseif k == "gi" then
            return function(vu)
                if mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, vu) or mt.ffc(lp.Character, vu) then
                    return true
                end
                for i, v in pairs(rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventoryWeapons")) do
                    if v["Name"] == vu then
                        return true
                    end
                end
                return false
            end
        elseif k == "tf" then
            return function(o, c)
                return table.find(o, c)
            end
        elseif k == "CheckBoss" then
            return function(boss)
                if mt.ffc(rt, boss) or mt.ffc(es, boss) then
                    return true
                end
                return false
            end
        elseif k == "IsHall" then
            return function()
                if mt.ffc(ws.Map, "IceCastle") then
                    if mt.ffc(ws.Map.IceCastle.Hall.LibraryDoor, "Keyhole") then
                        return true
                    end
                end
                return false
            end
        elseif k == "CheckBackpack" then
            return function(Item)
                if mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, Item) or mt.ffc(lp.Character, Item) then
                    return true
                end
                return false
            end
        elseif k == "GetMobRaid" then
            return function()
                local mobs = {}
                for _, v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                    if v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 and (lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 5000 then
                        table.insert(mobs, v)
                    end
                end
                return mobs
            end
        elseif k == "GetFruits" then
            return function()
                local results = {} 
                for _, v in pairs(rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")) do
                    if v.Type == "Blox Fruit" and v.Value <= 999999 then 
                        table.insert(results, {Name = v.Name, Value = v.Value})
                    end
                end
                return results
            end
        elseif k == "GetRaid" then
            return function(vu, mag)
                for _, v in pairs(ws["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:GetChildren()) do
                    if v:IsA('Part') or v:IsA('BasePart') then
                        if v.Name == vu and (v.Position-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= mag then
                            return v
                        end
                    end
                end
                return nil
            end
        elseif k == "GetType" then
            return function()
                local results = {} 
                for _, v in pairs(rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")) do
                    if v.Type == "Blox Fruit" then 
                        table.insert(results, v.Name)
                    end
                end
                return results
            end
        elseif k == "IsInList" then
            return function(list, item)
                for _, v in pairs(list) do
                    if v == item then
                        return true
                    end
                end
                return false
            end
        elseif k == "IsHeavenly" then
            return function()
                for _, v in pairs(rt:WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("CommF_"):InvokeServer("getTitles")) do
                    if v.Name == "Heavenly Devil" then
                        return true
                    end
                end
                return false
            end
        elseif k == "GetMonster" then
        	return function(vu)
                pcall(function()
                    for i,v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Model') and v:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 and (v.HumanoidRootPart.Position-game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= vu then
                            Monster = v
                            return
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
        elseif k == "GetMon_Soul" then
        	return function()
                for i,v in next,game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:GetChildren() do
                    if v.Name == "Living Zombie" then
                        table.insert(get_mon,v.Name)
                    end
                end
            end
        elseif k == "click" then
            return function(a)
                vim:SendMouseButtonEvent(a.AbsolutePosition.X+a.AbsoluteSize.X/2,a.AbsolutePosition.Y+90,0,true,a,1)
                vim:SendMouseButtonEvent(a.AbsolutePosition.X+a.AbsoluteSize.X/2,a.AbsolutePosition.Y+90,0,false,a,1)
            end
        elseif k == "HopLowServer" then
            return function(bO)
                pcall(function()
                    if not bO then
                        bO = 10
                    end
                    ticklon = tick()
                    repeat
                        task.wait()
                    until tick() - ticklon >= 1
                    local function Hop()
                        for r = 1, math.huge do
                            if ChooseRegion == nil or ChooseRegion == "" then
                                ChooseRegion = "Singapore"
                            else
                                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ServerBrowser.Frame.Filters.SearchRegion.TextBox.Text = ChooseRegion
                            end
                            local bP = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").__ServerBrowser:InvokeServer(r)
                            for k, v in pairs(bP) do
                                if k ~= game.JobId and v["Count"] < bO then
                                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").__ServerBrowser:InvokeServer("teleport", k)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        return false
                    end
                    if not getgenv().Loaded then
                        local function bQ(v)
                            if v.Name == "ErrorPrompt" then
                                if v.Visible then
                                    if v.TitleFrame.ErrorTitle.Text == "Teleport Failed" then
                                        HopLowServer()
                                        v.Visible = false
                                    end
                                end
                                v:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Visible"):Connect(
                                    function()
                                        if v.Visible then
                                            if v.TitleFrame.ErrorTitle.Text == "Teleport Failed" then
                                                HopLowServer()
                                                v.Visible = false
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                )
                            end
                        end
                        for k, v in pairs(game.CoreGui.RobloxPromptGui.promptOverlay:GetChildren()) do
                            bQ(v)
                        end
                        game.CoreGui.RobloxPromptGui.promptOverlay.ChildAdded:Connect(bQ)
                        getgenv().Loaded = true
                    end
                    while task.wait(0.1) do
                        Hop()
                    end
                end)
            end
        elseif k == "CheckItem" then
            return function(matname)
                for i,v in pairs(rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")) do
                    if type(v) == "table" then
                        if v.Type == "Material" then
                            if v.Name == matname then
                                return v.Count
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                return 0
            end
        elseif k == "FarmBone" then
            return function(tr)
                if tr then
                    if mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, "Fire Essence") or mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Fire Essence") then
                        repeat 
                            mt.Status(' Status : Use Fire Essence')
                            mt.Equip("Fire Essence")
                            mt.wt(.5)
                            rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyDragonTalon",true)
                            rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyDragonTalon")
                        until not mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, "Fire Essence") and not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Fire Essence")
                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyDragonTalon")
                        Dragon_Talon_C = true
                    else
                        if mt.ffc(es, "Demonic Soul") or mt.ffc(es, "Posessed Mummy") or mt.ffc(es, "Reborn Skeleton") or mt.ffc(es, "Living Zombie") then
                            for _, v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                                if v.Name == "Reborn Skeleton" or v.Name == "Living Zombie" or v.Name == "Demonic Soul" or v.Name == "Posessed Mummy" then
                                    if v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                        repeat mt.wt(.1)
											if mt.CheckItem('Bones') > 500 and rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Check") > 0 then
												repeat mt.wt(.2)
													rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Check")
													rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Buy",1,1)
												until rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Check") == 0
                                            end
                                            if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then
                                                lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Buso")
                                            end
                                            tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,30,0),1.5,200)
                                            Ew()
                                            mt.BN(v.Name)
                                        until not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                                    end
                                end 
                            end
                        else
                            tp(CFrame.new(-9505.8720703125, 172.10482788085938, 6158.9931640625),1.5)
                        end
                    end
                else
                    if mt.ffc(es, "Demonic Soul") or mt.ffc(es, "Posessed Mummy") or mt.ffc(es, "Reborn Skeleton") or mt.ffc(es, "Living Zombie") then
                        for _, v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                            if v.Name == "Reborn Skeleton" or v.Name == "Living Zombie" or v.Name == "Demonic Soul" or v.Name == "Posessed Mummy" then
                                if v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                    repeat mt.wt(.1)
                                        if mt.CheckItem('Bones') > 500 and rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Check") > 0 then
                                            repeat mt.wt(.2)
                                                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Check")
                                                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Buy",1,1)
                                            until rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones","Check") == 0
                                        end
                                        if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then
                                            lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Buso")
                                        end
                                        tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,30,0),1.5,200)
                                        Ew()
                                        mt.BN(v.Name)
                                    until not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                                end
                            end 
                        end
                    else
                        tp(CFrame.new(-9505.8720703125, 172.10482788085938, 6158.9931640625),1.5)
                    end
                end
            end
        elseif k == "Get_Item_Inventory" then
            return function(vu)
                if not mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, vu) and not  mt.ffc(lp.Character, vu) then
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LoadItem",tostring(vu))
                end
            end
elseif k == "BN" then
    return function(vName)
        pcall(function()

            local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer

            local function TweenObject(Object, Pos, Speed)
                Speed = Speed or 350
                if not Object or not Pos then return end
                local Distance = (Pos.Position - Object.Position).Magnitude
                local info = TweenInfo.new(Distance / Speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                local tween = TweenService:Create(Object, info, {CFrame = Pos})
                tween:Play()
            end

            local function GetMobPosition(EnemiesName)
                local pos = Vector3.zero
                local count = 0
                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == EnemiesName and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        pos += v.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                        count += 1
                    end
                end
                if count == 0 then return nil end
                return pos / count
            end
            

            local enemies = workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()
            if #enemies == 0 then return end

            local totalpos = {}
            for _, v in pairs(enemies) do
                if not totalpos[v.Name] then
                    totalpos[v.Name] = GetMobPosition(v.Name)
                end
            end

            pcall(function()
                sethiddenproperty(plr, "SimulationRadius", math.huge)
            end)
            

            for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                if v.Name == vName and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local hrp = v.HumanoidRootPart
                    local humanoid = v.Humanoid
                    
                    if humanoid.Health > 0 and (hrp.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 350 then
                        local mobPos = totalpos[v.Name]
                        if mobPos then
                            local TargetCFrame = CFrame.new(mobPos.X, mobPos.Y, mobPos.Z)
                            local Distance = (hrp.Position - TargetCFrame.Position).Magnitude
                            
                            if Distance > 3 and Distance <= 225 then
                                TweenObject(hrp, TargetCFrame, 300)
                                hrp.CanCollide = false
                                
                                if humanoid:FindFirstChild("Animator") then
                                    humanoid.Animator:Destroy()
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
    end
        elseif k == "Status" then
            return function(p)
                StatusFarmLabel.Text = "Status: " .. p
            end
        elseif k == "GetQuest" then
	        return function(vu)
                if (Vector3.new(-12379.1406, 601.433167, -6543.60742)-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 30 then
                    tp(CFrame.new(-12379.1406, 601.433167, -6543.60742),1.5)
                elseif (Vector3.new(-12379.1406, 601.433167, -6543.60742)-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 30 then
                    if vu == 'Good' then
                        repeat wait(.1)
                            tp(CFrame.new(-12392.5068, 603.319763, -6596.00586),1.5)
                        until (Vector3.new(-12392.5068, 603.319763, -6596.00586)-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3
                        wait(1)
                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest","Progress","Good")
                        wait(1)
                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest","StartTrial","Good")
                    elseif vu == 'Evil' then
                        repeat wait(.1)
                            tp(CFrame.new(-12392.2637, 603.319763, -6503.27832),1.5)
                        until (Vector3.new(-12392.2637, 603.319763, -6503.27832)-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3
                        wait(1)
                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest","Progress","Evil")
                        wait(1)
                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest","StartTrial","Evil")
                    end
                end
            end
        elseif k == "GetTorch" then
            return function(vu)
                repeat wait()
                    tp(ws.Map.HeavenlyDimension[vu].CFrame,1.5)
                until (ws.Map.HeavenlyDimension[vu].Position-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 7
                fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension[vu].ProximityPrompt)
                wait(0.5)
            end
        elseif k == "GetTorchX" then
            return function(vu)
                repeat wait()
                    tp(ws.Map.HellDimension[vu].CFrame,1.5)
                until (ws.Map.HellDimension[vu].Position-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 7
                fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.HellDimension[vu].ProximityPrompt)
                wait(0.5)
            end
        end
    end
})
local Players = game:GetService('Players')
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage')
local workspace = game:GetService('Workspace')
local Collection = {} Collection.__index = Collection
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.5) do
        mt.p(function()
            if lp.Data.Points.Value > 0 and lp.Data.Stats["Melee"].Level.Value < 2650 then
                ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Melee", lp.Data.Points.Value)
            end
            if lp.Data.Stats["Melee"].Level.Value >= 2650 and lp.Data.Points.Value > 0 and lp.Data.Stats["Defense"].Level.Value < 2550 then
                ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Defense", lp.Data.Points.Value)
            end
            if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then
                ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Buso")
            end
        end)
    end
end)
getgenv()['Fast Attack'] = true
local w = 0

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(w) do
        if getgenv()['Fast Attack'] and not Stop_Fast_Attack then
            if mt.sf(lp.PlayerGui.Main.Version.Text, "v26.6.1") then
                xpcall(function()
                    if (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool') 
                    and (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid') 
                    and (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()).Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                        
                        for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                            if v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid') and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') then
                                if (v.HumanoidRootPart.Position - LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 60 then
                                    
                                    if (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):FindFirstChild('Stun') then
                                        (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()).Stun.Value = 0
                                    end
                                    if (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):FindFirstChild('Busy') then
                                        (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()).Busy.Value = false
                                    end
                                    if v:FindFirstChild('Stun') then
                                        v.Stun.Value = 0
                                    end
                                    if v:FindFirstChild('Busy') then
                                        v.Busy.Value = false
                                    end
                                    if rt.Modules.Net:FindFirstChild('RE') and rt.Modules.Net.RE:FindFirstChild('RegisterHit') then
                                        rt.Modules.Net.RE.RegisterHit:SetAttribute('Virtual', not rt.Modules.Net.RE.RegisterHit:GetAttribute('Virtual'))
                                    end
                                    if LocalPlayer.Character then
                                        LocalPlayer.Character:SetAttribute('Clashable', not LocalPlayer.Character:GetAttribute('Clashable'))
                                    end
                                    local nearbyCount = 0
                                    for _, y in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                                        if y:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid') and y.Humanoid.Health > 0 and y:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') 
                                        and (y.HumanoidRootPart.Position - LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 60 then
                                            nearbyCount = nearbyCount + 1

                                            if nearbyCount > 5 then
                                                w = 0.1
                                            elseif nearbyCount > 2 and nearbyCount <= 5 then
                                                w = 0.03
                                            else
                                                w = 0
                                            end

                                            r_Net_0:RemoteEvent("RegisterAttack"):FireServer(math.huge)
                                            r_Net_0:RemoteEvent("RegisterHit", true):FireServer(
                                                y.Head,
                                                {{y, y.Head}, y.Head},
                                                nil,
                                                tostring(LocalPlayer.UserId):sub(2, 4) .. tostring(coroutine.running()):sub(11, 15)
                                            )
                                        end
                                    end

                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end,warn)
            else
                assert(getrenv, "Exploit not supported")
                local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
                local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                local Players = game:GetService("Players")
                local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
                local registerHit = debug.getupvalue(getrenv()._G.SendHitsToServer, 1)
                local registerAttack = ReplicatedStorage.Modules.Net["RE/RegisterAttack"]
                local function GetClosestEnemies()
                    local enemies = CollectionService:GetTagged("BasicMob")
                    if #enemies == 0 then
                        return nil
                    end
                    local validEnemies = {}
                    local playerPosition = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character.PrimaryPart.Position
                    if not playerPosition then
                        return nil
                    end
                    for _, mob in pairs(enemies) do
                        local humanoid = mob:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        local primaryPart = mob.PrimaryPart
                        if humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 and primaryPart then
                            local distance = (primaryPart.Position - playerPosition).Magnitude
                            if distance <= 100 then
                                validEnemies[#validEnemies + 1] = {
                                    mob = mob,
                                    distance = distance,
                                }
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if #validEnemies == 0 then
                        return nil
                    end
                    table.sort(validEnemies, function(a, b)
                        return a.distance < b.distance
                    end)
                    return #validEnemies > 2 and { validEnemies[1], validEnemies[2] } or validEnemies
                end

                local function Attack()
                    local enemies = GetClosestEnemies()
                    if not enemies then
                        return
                    end
                    local hitData = {}
                    for _, enemy in pairs(enemies) do
                        local rootPart = enemy.mob:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if rootPart then
                            hitData[#hitData + 1] = { enemy.mob, rootPart }
                        end
                    end
                    if #hitData > 0 then
                        registerAttack:FireServer(0 / 0)
                        coroutine.resume(registerHit, hitData[1][2], { table.unpack(hitData, 2) })
                    end
                end

                local Passed, Statement = pcall(function()
                    Attack()
                end)

                if not Passed then
                    warn("Error in Combat script: " .. tostring(Statement))
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

    if v.Type == 'Material' then
        if v.Name == 'Mirror Fractal' then
            Mirror_Fractal_H = true
        end
    end
end

local function FarmLevel()
    if Three_World then
        if tostring(string.match(tostring(rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CakePrinceSpawner")), "%d+")) == 'nil' or tostring(string.match(tostring(rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CakePrinceSpawner")), "%d+")) == nil then
            rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CakePrinceSpawner",true)
        end
    end 
    if Three_World then
        if mt.ffc(es, "Cake Prince") or  mt.ffc(rt, "Cake Prince") then
            if mt.ffc(es, "Cake Prince") then
                for _,v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "Cake Prince" and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                        repeat mt.wt()
                            if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then
                                lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Buso")
                            end
                            tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,-30,0),1.5)
                            
                            Ew()
                            StatusItemLabel.Text = " Attacking Cake Prince"
                        until not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not getgenv().AutoFarm
                    end
                end
            elseif mt.ffc(rt, "Cake Prince") then
                for _,v in pairs(rt:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "Cake Prince" and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                        repeat mt.wt()
                            if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then
                                lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Buso")
                            end
                            tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,-30,0),1.5)
                            Ew()
                            StatusItemLabel.Text = " Attacking Cake Prince"
                        until not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not getgenv().AutoFarm
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    if Three_World then
        if es:FindFirstChild('rip_indra True Form') or rt:FindFirstChild('rip_indra True Form') then
            if not rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TushitaProgress")['OpenedDoor'] then

            else
                tp(CFrame.new(-2091.911865234375, 70.00884246826172, -12142.8359375),1.5)
            end
        end
    end
end

local function Get()
    if not noFruit then
        for _, fruitTool in pairs(lp.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
            if fruitTool:GetAttribute("OriginalName") ~= nil and mt.sf(fruitTool.Name, "Fruit") and fruitTool:IsA("Tool") and not mt.IsInList(mt.GetType(), fruitTool:GetAttribute("OriginalName")) then
                local args = {
                    "StoreFruit",
                    fruitTool:GetAttribute("OriginalName"),
                    fruitTool
                }
                rt:WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("CommF_"):InvokeServer(unpack(args))
                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetFruits", false)
            end
        end
        for _, fruitTool in pairs(lp.Character:GetChildren()) do
            if fruitTool:GetAttribute("OriginalName") ~= nil and mt.sf(fruitTool.Name, "Fruit") and fruitTool:IsA("Tool") and not mt.IsInList(mt.GetType(), fruitTool:GetAttribute("OriginalName")) then
                local args = {
                    "StoreFruit",
                    fruitTool:GetAttribute("OriginalName"),
                    fruitTool
                }
                rt:WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("CommF_"):InvokeServer(unpack(args))
                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetFruits", false)
            end
        end
    end
end
_G.Ew = true
Ewx = true
local q
task.spawn(function()
    while mt.wt() do
        if _G.Ew then
            Ew()
        else
            Get()
            if Ewx then
                q = 0
            else
                q = 0.2
            end
        end
    end
end)
task.spawn(function()
    while mt.wt(1) do
        xpcall(function()
            if not Black_Leg_C then
                repeat mt.wt(q)
                    if not God_Human_C_M then 
                    if Old_World then
                    if Beli.Value >= 150000 then
                        StatusFarmLabel.Text = "Status: Buying Black Leg"
                    tp(CFrame.new(-983.566895, 13.2651796, 3990.49951))
                    
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBlackLeg")
                    end
                    Ew()
                    mt.wt(0.05)
                end
                end
                    if mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Black Leg") or mt.ffc(lp.Backpack, "Black Leg") and not Black_Leg_C then
                        Black_Leg_C = true 
                        mt.Equip("Black Leg")
                    end
                until Black_Leg_C
            end
            if not Electro_C then
                
                repeat mt.wt(q)
                    
                    Ew()
                    if Beli.Value >= 500000 then
                    vim:SendKeyEvent(true, "V", false, game)
                    wait(.5)
                    vim:SendKeyEvent(false, "V", false, game)
                    if mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Black Leg") and lp.Character["Black Leg"].Level.Value >= 300 and not Electro_C then
                        if lp.Character["Black Leg"].Level.Value >= 400 then
                            Black_Leg_C_M = true
                        end
                        Electro_C = true 
                        mt.wt(0.05)
                        if Old_World then
                        tp(CFrame.new(-5382.7417, 13.317874, -2148.80347))
                        end
                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyElectro")
                    end
                end
                until Electro_C 
            end
            if not Fishman_Karate_C then
                repeat mt.wt(q)       
                    Ew()
                    if mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Electro") and lp.Character["Electro"].Level.Value >= 300 and not Fishman_Karate_C then
                        if lp.Character["Electro"].Level.Value >= 400 then
                            Electro_C_M = true
                        end
                        Fishman_Karate_C = true 
                        mt.wt(0.05)
                        if Old_World then
                            if (CFrame.new(61164, 12, 1820).Position - lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude >= 2000 then
                            lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(61164, 12, 1820)
                            end
                        end
                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyFishmanKarate")
                    end
                until Fishman_Karate_C
            end
            if not Fishman_Karate_C_M then
                repeat task.wait(q)
                    Ew()
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyFishmanKarate")
                    local dc = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Fishman Karate")
                    if dc and dc:FindFirstChild("Level") and dc.Level.Value >= 400 then
                        Fishman_Karate_C_M = true
                    end
                until Fishman_Karate_C_M
            end
            mt.wt(q)
            if not Dragon_Claw_C then
                
                local result = rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BlackbeardReward","DragonClaw","2")
                if result == 1 or result == 2 then
                    pcall(function()
                        if lp.Character["Fishman Karate"].Level.Value >= 400 then
                            Fishman_Karate_C_M = true
                        end
                    end)
                    Dragon_Claw_C = true
                end
            end
            repeat task.wait(q)
                Ew()
                if not Super_human then
                    if Dragon_Claw_C then
                        if mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Dragon Claw") and lp.Character["Dragon Claw"].Level.Value >= 300 then
                            if lp.Character["Dragon Claw"].Level.Value >= 400 then
                                Dragon_Claw_C_M = true
                            end
                            local args = {
                                [1] = "BuySuperhuman"
                            }
                            if rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack(args)) == 1 or rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack(args)) == 2 then
                                Super_human = true
                                if lp.Character["Superhuman"].Level.Value >= 400 then
                                    Super_humanw_C_M = true
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            until Super_human
            if not Death_Step then
                if rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyDeathStep") == 1 or rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyDeathStep") == 2 then
                    Death_Step = true
                end
            end
            if Black_Leg_C_M then
                repeat task.wait(q)
                    Ew()
                    local ds = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Death Step")
                    if ds and ds:FindFirstChild("Level") and ds.Level.Value >= 400 then


                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBlackLeg")
                        local bl = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Black Leg")
                        if bl and bl:FindFirstChild("Level") and bl.Level.Value >= 400 then
                            Black_Leg_C_M = true
                        end
                    end
                until Black_Leg_C_M
            end
            if not Death_Step_C_M then
                repeat task.wait(q)
                    Ew()
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyDeathStep")
                    local ds = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Death Step")
                    if ds and ds:FindFirstChild("Level") and ds.Level.Value >= 400 then
                        Death_Step_C_M = true
                    end
                until Death_Step_C_M
            end
            if not Electro_C_M then
                repeat task.wait(q)
                    Ew()
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyElectro")
                    local elec = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Electro")
                    if elec and elec:FindFirstChild("Level") and elec.Level.Value >= 400 then
                        Electro_C_M = true
                    end
                until Electro_C_M
            end
            if not Fishman_Karate_C_M then
                repeat task.wait(q)
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyFishmanKarate")
                    warn()
                    local fm = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Fishman Karate")

                        Dragon_Claw_C_M = true
                    end
                until Dragon_Claw_C_M
            end
            if not Sharkman_Karate_C then

                    end

            end
            if not Sharkman_Karate_C_M then
                repeat task.wait(q)
                    Ew()
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuySharkmanKarate")
                    local dc = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Sharkman Karate")
                    if dc and dc:FindFirstChild("Level") and dc.Level.Value >= 400 then
                        Sharkman_Karate_C_M = true
                    end
                until Sharkman_Karate_C_M
            end
            if not Electric_Claw_C then
                repeat task.wait(q)
                    if rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyElectricClaw") == 1 or rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyElectricClaw") == 2 then
                        Electric_Claw_C = true
                    end
                until Electric_Claw_C
            end
            if not Electric_Claw_C_M then

        end,warn)
    end

local function CHECKCDKQUEST()
    if not mt.gi("Cursed Dual Katana") then
        if mt.gi("Tushita") and mt.gi("Yama") then
            local Inventory = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")
            for _, v in pairs(Inventory) do
                if v.Type == "Sword" then
                    if v.Name == "Tushita" and v.Mastery >= 400 then
                        Tushita_M = true
                    elseif v.Name == "Yama" and v.Mastery >= 400 then
                        Yama_M = true
                    end
                end
            end
            return Tushita_M and Yama_M
        end
    end
    return false
end

                    end

                            Quest = "Gravity Blade"
                            return
                        end

                            Quest = "Longsword"
                            return
                        end

                            until (lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position-Vector3.new(6377.12549, 296.634735, -6843.76025)).Magnitude <= 1 or not mt.IsHall() or not getgenv().AutoFarm
                            mt.wt(1)

                                                mt.Status(' Status : Farm Raid')

                                                        tp(mt.GetRaid('Island 3',2500).CFrame*CFrame.new(0,120,0),1.5)
                                                    elseif mt.GetRaid('Island 2',2500) ~= nil then

                                                        tp(mt.GetRaid('Island 1',2500).CFrame*CFrame.new(0,120,0),1.5)
                                                    end

                                                                            v:Destroy()
                                                                        end
                                                                    end

                                                                local offset
                                                                if RandomTween == 1 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(0, 30, 1)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 2 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(0, 30, 15)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 3 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(1, 30, -15)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 4 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(15, 30, 0)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 5 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(-15, 30, 0)
                                                                end
                                                                tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*offset,1.5)
                                                                if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then

                                                            until not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or #mt.GetMobRaid() == 0
                                                        end
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            else

                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Magma-Magma" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Magma"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Rumble-Rumble" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Rumble"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Flame-Flame" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Flame"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Ice-Ice" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Ice"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Light-Light" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Light"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "String-String" then

                        local function CheckFruit()
                            for i, v in pairs(rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")) do
                                if v["Value"] and v["Value"] >= 1000000 then
                                    return true
                                end
                            end
                            return false
