                                                    if Select_Map == "Magma" or Select_Map == "Flame" then
                                                        for i, v in pairs(ws:GetDescendants()) do
                                                            if v.Name == "Lava" then
                                                                v:Destroy()
                                                            end
                                                        end
                                                    end
                                                    if mt.GetRaid('Island 5',2500) ~= nil then
                                                        tp(mt.GetRaid('Island 5',2500).CFrame*CFrame.new(0,120,0),1.5)
                                                    elseif mt.GetRaid('Island 4',2500) ~= nil then
                                                        tp(mt.GetRaid('Island 4',2500).CFrame*CFrame.new(0,120,0),1.5)
                                                    elseif mt.GetRaid('Island 3',2500) ~= nil then
                                                        tp(mt.GetRaid('Island 3',2500).CFrame*CFrame.new(0,120,0),1.5)
                                                    elseif mt.GetRaid('Island 2',2500) ~= nil then
                                                        tp(mt.GetRaid('Island 2',2500).CFrame*CFrame.new(0,120,0),1.5)
                                                    elseif mt.GetRaid('Island 1',2500) ~= nil then
                                                        tp(mt.GetRaid('Island 1',2500).CFrame*CFrame.new(0,120,0),1.5)
                                                    end
                                                else
                                                    for _, v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                                                        if v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid").Health > 0 and (lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position).Magnitude <= 5000 then
                                                            repeat mt.wt(.1)
                                                                if Select_Map == "Magma" or Select_Map == "Flame" then
                                                                    for i, v in pairs(ws:GetDescendants()) do
                                                                        if v.Name == "Lava" then
                                                                            v:Destroy()
                                                                        end
                                                                    end
                                                                end
                                                                local RandomTween = math.random(1, 5)
                                                                local offset
                                                                if RandomTween == 1 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(0, 30, 1)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 2 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(0, 30, 15)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 3 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(1, 30, -15)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 4 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(15, 30, 0)
                                                                elseif RandomTween == 5 then
                                                                    offset = CFrame.new(-15, 30, 0)
                                                                end
                                                                tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*offset,1.5)
                                                                if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then
                                                                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Buso")
                                                                end
                                                                Ew()
                                                            until not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or #mt.GetMobRaid() == 0
                                                        end
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            else
                                                if lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Dark-Dark" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Dark"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Sand-Sand" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Sand"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Magma-Magma" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Magma"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Rumble-Rumble" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Rumble"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Flame-Flame" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Flame"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Ice-Ice" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Ice"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Light-Light" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Light"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "String-String" then
                                                    Select_Map = "String"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Quake-Quake" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Quake"
                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Buddha-Buddha" then
                                                    Select_Map = "Buddha"
                                                else
                                                    Select_Map = "Ice"
                                                end
                                                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("RaidsNpc", "Select",Select_Map)
                                                mt.wt(0.2)
                                                if lp.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Special Microchip') or lp.Character:FindFirstChild('Special Microchip') and lp.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                                    if pi == 4442272183 and lp.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                                        fireclickdetector(ws.Map.CircleIsland.RaidSummon2.Button.Main.ClickDetector, 1)
                                                        local pt = 0
                                                        repeat 
                                                            pt = pt+1
                                                            mt.wt(1)
                                                        until pt >= 20 or lp.PlayerGui.Main.Timer.Visible
                                                    elseif pi == 7449423635 then
                                                        tp(CFrame.new(-5034, 315, -2951),1.5)
                                                        if (CFrame.new(-5034, 315, -2951).Position-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3 then
                                                            if lp.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                                                fireclickdetector(ws.Map["Boat Castle"].RaidSummon2.Button.Main.ClickDetector, 1)
                                                                local pt = 0
                                                                repeat 
                                                                    pt = pt+1
                                                                    mt.wt(1)
                                                                until pt >= 20 or lp.PlayerGui.Main.Timer.Visible
                                                            end
                                                        end
                                                    end
                                                else
                                                    if not lp.PlayerGui.Main.TopHUDList.RaidTimer.Visible then
                                                        if lp.Data.Fragments.Value >= 5000 then
                                                            if lp.Data.Beli.Value >= 3000000 then
                                                                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyGodHuman")
                                                                God_Human_C = true
                                                                return
                                                            end
                                                            return
                                                        end
                                                        table.sort(mt.GetFruits(), function(a, b)
                                                            if a.Value < 100000 and a.Value < 100000 then
                                                                return a.Value < b.Value
                                                            end
                                                        end)
                                                        mt.wt(1)
                                                        if #mt.GetFruits() > 0 and not God_Human_C then
                                                            warn()
                                                            mt.wt(2)
                                                            if not lp.PlayerGui.Main.TopHUDList.RaidTimer.Visible then
                                                                if lp.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 and lp.Data.Fragments.Value < 5000 then
                                                                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LoadFruit", mt.GetFruits()[1].Name)
                                                                elseif Fragments.Value < 5000 then 
                                                                    break
                                                                end
                                                                if lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Dark-Dark" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Dark"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Sand-Sand" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Sand"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Magma-Magma" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Magma"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Rumble-Rumble" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Rumble"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Flame-Flame" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Flame"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Ice-Ice" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Ice"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Light-Light" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Light"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "String-String" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "String"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Quake-Quake" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Quake"
                                                                elseif lp.Data.DevilFruit.Value == "Buddha-Buddha" then
                                                                    Select_Map = "Buddha"
                                                                else
                                                                    Select_Map = "Ice"
                                                                end
                                                                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("RaidsNpc", "Select",Select_Map)
                                                                if pi == 4442272183 and lp.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                                                    fireclickdetector(ws.Map.CircleIsland.RaidSummon2.Button.Main.ClickDetector, 1)
                                                                    local pt = 0
                                                                    repeat 
                                                                        pt = pt+1
                                                                        mt.wt(1)
                                                                    until pt >= 20 or lp.PlayerGui.Main.Timer.Visible
                                                                elseif pi == 7449423635 then
                                                                    tp(CFrame.new(-5034, 315, -2951),1.5)
                                                                    if (CFrame.new(-5034, 315, -2951).Position-lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3 then
                                                                        if lp.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                                                            fireclickdetector(ws.Map["Boat Castle"].RaidSummon2.Button.Main.ClickDetector, 1)
                                                                            local pt = 0
                                                                            repeat 
                                                                                pt = pt+1
                                                                                mt.wt(1)
                                                                            until pt >= 20 or lp.PlayerGui.Main.Timer.Visible
                                                                        end
                                                                    end
                                                                end
                                                            end
                                                        else
                                                            Quest = nil
                                                            mt.Status(' Auto Farm Level')
                                                            FarmLevel()
                                                            StatusItemLabel.Text = "Attack Mob : " .. tostring(NameEnemy)
                                                        end
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                until God_Human_C
                            end
                            return
                        end
                        if Level.Value >= 700 and not New_World and not Three_World then
                            Quest = "World 2"
                            return
                        end
                        if New_World and CheckFindWaterKey and Level.Value >= 1500 and rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TalkTrevor","1") == 0 and not mt.IsHall() and mt.IsHeavenly() then
                            Quest = "TravelZou"
                            return
                        end
                        Quest = nil
                        mt.Status(' Auto Farm Level')
                        FarmLevel()
                        StatusItemLabel.Text = "Attack Mob : " .. tostring(NameEnemy)
                    end
                end
            end
        end,warn)
    end
end)
task.spawn(function()
    while mt.wt() do
        xpcall(function()
            if Quest ~= nil then
                mt.Status(Quest)
            end
            if Quest == "Saber" then
                if not old_World then
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelMain")
                end
                local Q_Saber = rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress")
                if Q_Saber["UsedTorch"] == false then
                    for _, v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Map.Jungle.QuestPlates:GetChildren()) do
                        if table.find({"Plate1", "Plate2", "Plate3", "Plate4", "Plate5"}, v.Name) then
                            v.Button.CFrame = lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        end
                    end
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "GetTorch")
                    mt.Equip("Torch")
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "DestroyTorch")
                elseif Q_Saber["UsedCup"] == false then
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "GetCup")
                    mt.Equip("Cup")
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "FillCup", game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Cup)
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "SickMan")
                elseif Q_Saber["KilledMob"] == false then
                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon")
                    local MobLeader = mt.ffc(es, "Mob Leader")
                    if MobLeader then
                        for _, v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                            if v.Name == "Mob Leader" then
                                repeat mt.wt()
                                    tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0),1.5)
                                    if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "HasBuso") then
                                        rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Buso")
                                    end
                                    Ew()
                                until not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or mt.gi("Saber")
                                rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon")
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        tp(CFrame.new(-2848.59399, 7.4272871, 5342.44043),1.5)
                    end

                    rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon")

task.spawn(function()
    while mt.wt() do
        xpcall(function()
            for _, v in pairs(es:GetChildren()) do
                if mt.ffc(v, "Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 and mt.ffc(v, "HumanoidRootPart") then
                    if v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 then
                        v:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
            if mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Black Leg") then
                vim:SendKeyEvent(true, "V", false, game)
                mt.wt(0.1)
                vim:SendKeyEvent(false, "V", false, game)
            end
            if mt.ffc(lp.Character,"HumanoidRootPart") and not mt.ffc(lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart,"Lock") then
                local humanoid = lp.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                if humanoid and humanoid.Sit then
                    humanoid.Sit = false
                end
                local Noclip = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
                Noclip.Name = "Lock"
                Noclip.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1e9, 1e9, 1e9)
                Noclip.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                Noclip.P = 1e4
                Noclip.Parent = lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            end
        end,warn)
    end
end)
task.spawn(function()
    while mt.wt(1) do
        pcall(function()
            if not mt.ffc(lp.Character, "Highlight") then
                local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
                highlight.Name = "Highlight"
                highlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(251, 97, 43) 
                highlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(251, 97, 43)
                highlight.FillTransparency = 1
                highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
                highlight.Adornee = lp.Character
                highlight.Parent = lp.Character
            end
        end)
    end
end)

local ps = game:GetService("Players")
local lp = ps.LocalPlayer
local function waitForCharacter()
    while not lp.Character or not lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") do
        task.wait(0.5)
    end
    return lp.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
end
local lastPosition = waitForCharacter().Position
local stayTime = 0
local checkInterval = 1
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        if Quest ~= "Cursed Dual Katana" and Quest ~= "Evo Race V2" and Quest ~= "Evo Race V1" and not SROP then
            task.wait(checkInterval)
            local currentPosition = waitForCharacter().Position
            local distance = (currentPosition - lastPosition).Magnitude
            if distance <= 1 then
                stayTime = stayTime + checkInterval
                if stayTime >= 30 and Quest ~= "Cursed Dual Katana" and Quest ~= "Evo Race V2" and Quest ~= "Evo Race V1" and not SROP then
                    mt.HopLowServer(9)
                end
            else
                stayTime = 0
                lastPosition = currentPosition
            end
        end
    end
end)

    while task.wait() do
        if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("Heavenly") then
            fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension["Torch1"].ProximityPrompt)
            fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension["Torch2"].ProximityPrompt)

            fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.HellDimension["Torch2"].ProximityPrompt)
            fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.HellDimension["Torch3"].ProximityPrompt)
        end
    end
end)

local function checkstatus()
    pcall(function()
        local lv = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Data.Level.Value
        local frags = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Data.Fragments.Value
        local beli = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Data.Beli.Value
        local race = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Data.Race.Value
        local sea = "1"
        if lv > 1550 then sea = "3" elseif lv > 700 then sea = "2" end
        
        -- Update Dashboard Stats
        LvlDashboardLabel.Text = "Level : " .. lv .. "    Third Sea : " .. (lv > 1550 and "✅" or "❌")
        FragDashboardLabel.Text = "Frag : " .. frags
        BeliDashboardLabel.Text = "Beli : " .. beli
        RaceDashboardLabel.Text = "Race : " .. race
        
        local pullLV = rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CheckTempleDoor")
        LeverDashboardLabel.Text = (pullLV and "🟢" or "🔴") .. " Pull Lever"
        
        -- Optimization: Fetch inventory once to reduce server calls
        local inventory = rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")
        local char = lp.Character
        local backpack = lp.Backpack
        
        local function hasItem(name, itemType)
            if char:FindFirstChild(name) or backpack:FindFirstChild(name) then return true end
            if inventory and type(inventory) == "table" then
                for _, v in pairs(inventory) do
                    if v.Name == name and (not itemType or v.Type == itemType) then
                        return true
                    end
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        local function checkMaterial(name)
            if inventory and type(inventory) == "table" then
                for _, v in pairs(inventory) do
                    if v.Name == name and v.Type == "Material" then
                        return v.Count or 1
                    end
                end
            end
            return 0
        end

        local ghmStatus = rt.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyGodhuman")
        local isGHMOwned = (ghmStatus == 1 or ghmStatus == 2)
        
        -- Update Dashboard Items
        GHMDashboardLabel.Text = (isGHMOwned and "🟢" or "🔴") .. " GodHuman"
        CDKDashboardLabel.Text = (hasItem("Cursed Dual Katana", "Sword") and "🟢" or "🔴") .. " Curse Dual Katana"
        MirrorDashboardLabel.Text = (checkMaterial("Mirror Fractal") >= 1 and "🟢" or "🔴") .. " Mirror Fractal"
        GuitarDashboardLabel.Text = (mt.gi("Skull Guitar") and "🟢" or "🔴") .. " Skull Guitar"
        ValkDashboardLabel.Text = (mt.gi("Valkyrie Helm") and "🟢" or "🔴") .. " Valkyrie Helm"
    end)
end

task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        checkstatus()
        task.wait(2)
    end
end)
StatusItemLabel.Text = "Status: Loaded Successfully "
wait(10)
StatusItemLabel.Text = "Kaitun Blox Fruit by Kemu Hub "

loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/tokaruun/script/refs/heads/main/attack.lua"))()
notify("Kemu Hub", "Loaded Successfully", 3)
